<div class="form_block_posted">
<a id="section84"></a><div class="form_title"><div class="form_title_left"><img title="Display" alt="Display" src="icons/32x32_tp/display.png"></div><div class="form_title_center"><h4>Display<img title="All parameters that related to display" alt="All parameters that related to display" src="icons/10x10/info_gray.gif">
</h4></div>
<div class="form_title_right"><button type="submit"  formaction="index.php?m=device&s=query#section84" name="collapse_section84"><img title="Collapse Display" alt="Collapse box" src="icons/16x16_tp/arrow_up2.png"></button></div>
</div>
<div class="form_item">
<img title="Number of horizontal pixels in one row. The distance measured between the furthest corners of the display. In case of display with rounded edges this refers to the smallest bounding rectangle." alt="Number of horizontal pixels in one row. The distance measured between the furthest corners of the display.
